[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the shadowsocks JSON [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing functionality. The issue occurs when the `json_parse_ex` function attempts [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto read [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte beyond the allocated heap buffer boundary at line [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m`. This is a memory safety vulnerability with a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, classified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a READ [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that attempts to access memory [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte beyond the allocated heap region. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer has classified this as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow with a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during fuzzing operations with the following [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacteristics:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Access Violation**: The invalid read occurs at address [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b7[0m[39m`, which is located exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte heap region [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x5020000000b7[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This indicates an off-by-one error where the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode attempts to read one byte past the end of the allocated buffer.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following execution [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `[0m[35m/src/[0m[95mjson_fuzz.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m12[0m[39m` - Entry point for the fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `json_parse` in `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m958[0m[39m` - High-level JSON parsing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `json_parse_ex` in `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m310:45[0m[39m` - Low-level parsing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction where the actual overflow occurs[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory State**: The shadow bytes analysis reveals:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The region shows `[0m[1;36m07[0m[39m` at the buggy address, indicating [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes are partially [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressable[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The memory is surrounded by heap left redzones [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fa`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which are protective [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzones placed by the memory allocator[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocation suggests the parser is handling a relatively small input[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Allocation Details**: The [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer was allocated through the standard [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory allocation path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`malloc` → `operator new`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating this is likely a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate heap allocation for processing input data.[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m310[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b2 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m309[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b3 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m310[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b4 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:323[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m323[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m:                            [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m325[0m[39m:                            [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b2 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m326[0m[39m:                            [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b3 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[39m:                            [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b4 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability** in the JSON parser's unicode escape sequence[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling. The issue occurs at two locations in `src/json.c`:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprimary vulnerability location reported[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Basic unicode escape [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\uXXXX` processing[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39msecondary vulnerability not mentioned in evaluation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Surrogate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpair `\uXXXX\uXXXX` processing[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe provided `good_patch.diff` only fixes line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m but leaves line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m vulnerable [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the same off-by-one error.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Root Cause[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability stems from an **off-by-one error in boundary checking** when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing the pre-increment-then-dereference pattern `*++ state.ptr`:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The operator `*++ ptr` first increments the pointer, then dereferences it[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. When exactly N bytes remain and the code performs N `*++ state.ptr` operations, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe last operation increments the pointer to equal `end`, then dereferences it, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read beyond the buffer[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The boundary checks use `end - state.ptr < N` which should be `end - state.ptr <[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Example for line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallows exactly [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes remaining[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Operations: [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m × `*++ state.ptr` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m310[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Result: After [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m increments, `state.ptr == end`, and dereferencing reads [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpast the buffer[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Changes Required [0m[1;39m([0m[39mApplied to Initial Codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBasic Unicode Escape[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m File: src/json.c, line [0m[1;36m306[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** This ensures that when processing `\uXXXX`, there are at least [0m[1;36m5[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes remaining [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent position + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so after [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m increments, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`state.ptr` is still less than `end`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSurrogate Pair Unicode Escape[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m File: src/json.c, line [0m[1;36m323[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** This ensures that when processing surrogate pairs [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\uXXXX\uXXXX`, there are at least [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes remaining [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent position + [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters: `\`, `u`, and [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so after [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m increments, `state.ptr` is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill less than `end`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBoth changes are minimal, surgical modifications that:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserve existing logic:** The parser's two-pass architecture, string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling, UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m encoding, and all other functionality remains unchanged[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follow established patterns:** The fixes align with the correct boundary [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking patterns already present in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m633[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Address the complete vulnerability:** Unlike the incomplete `good_patch.diff`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis fixes both vulnerable locations[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes:** Only two integer constants are modified, reducing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregression risk[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent with Codebase Patterns:** Similar boundary checks for [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"false"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m633[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already use this correct pattern[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Complete Fix:** Addresses both the primary vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m306[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecondary vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m323[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that the good patch missed[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes:** The parser still correctly processes all valid JSON, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluding unicode escapes and surrogate pairs[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Memory Safety:** Eliminates the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte heap buffer over-read [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Fixes the reported crash:** The AddressSanitizer-detected heap-buffer-overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m is prevented by the line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m fix[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Prevents similar crashes:** The line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m fix prevents analogous crashes with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate pair inputs[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Maintains functionality:** All valid JSON inputs continue to parse correctly[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No impact on fuzzing:** The harness code remains unchanged; the fuzzer can [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue testing with the same logic[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected for valid inputs[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Invalid inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincomplete unicode escapes at buffer boundaries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly fail with error messages instead of crashing[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Recommendations:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify unicode escape sequences: `[0m[32m"\u0000"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"\uFFFF"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"\u1234"[0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify surrogate pairs: `[0m[32m"\uD800\uDC00"[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mU+[0m[1;36m10000[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test boundary conditions with crafted inputs[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Run existing JSON parser test suite to ensure no regressions[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use AddressSanitizer during testing to confirm the fix[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates the correct pattern for boundary checking with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple pre-increment operations:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m603[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparsing [0m[32m"true"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` with [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m × `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ✓[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m620[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparsing [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` with [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m × `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ✓[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m634[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparsing [0m[32m"null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` with [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m × `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ✓[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese examples confirm that the pattern `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < N` for N increments is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe established correct approach in this codebase. The unicode escape handlers were[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimply missing the +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m adjustment that these other sections have correct.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
